## Diagram 1

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    Start([Component Rendered]) --> CheckShow{show prop true?}
    CheckShow -->|Yes| SyncState[Sync subscription state to local]
    CheckShow -->|No| End([Modal Hidden])
    
    SyncState --> CheckMode{subscriptionDetails exists?}
    CheckMode -->|Yes| SetUpdate[Set mode to UPDATE]
    CheckMode -->|No| SetSave[Set mode to SAVE]
    
    SetUpdate --> PopulateUpdate[Populate with existing data]
    SetSave --> PopulateNew[Populate with defaults]
    
    PopulateUpdate --> RenderModal[Render Modal UI]
    PopulateNew --> RenderModal
    
    RenderModal --> UserInteract[User interacts with form]
    UserInteract --> ToggleEmail[Toggle Email checkbox]
    UserInteract --> ToggleSMS[Toggle SMS checkbox]
    UserInteract --> TogglePlatform[Toggle Platform checkbox]
    UserInteract --> EditEmail[Edit email input]
    UserInteract --> EditPhone[Edit phone input]
    
    ToggleEmail --> ValidateChanges{Validate form}
    ToggleSMS --> ValidateChanges
    TogglePlatform --> ValidateChanges
    EditEmail --> ValidateChanges
    EditPhone --> ValidateChanges
    
    ValidateChanges -->|Invalid| DisableSave[Disable Save button]
    ValidateChanges -->|Valid & Changed| EnableSave[Enable Save button]
    ValidateChanges -->|No changes| DisableSave
    
    EnableSave --> UserClicksSave[User clicks Save]
    UserClicksSave --> CheckOptIn{isOptIn?}
    
    CheckOptIn -->|Yes| SetApproval[Set requires_approval]
    CheckOptIn -->|No| CheckSaveMode{Check mode}
    SetApproval --> CheckSaveMode
    
    CheckSaveMode -->|UPDATE & all disabled| CallUnsubscribe[Call unsubscribe API]
    CheckSaveMode -->|SAVE| CallSubscribe[Call subscribe API]
    CheckSaveMode -->|UPDATE| CallUpdate[Call updateSubscription API]
    
    CallUnsubscribe --> ShowAlert[Show success/error alert]
    CallSubscribe --> ShowAlert
    CallUpdate --> ShowAlert
    
    ShowAlert --> UserDismiss{User action}
    UserDismiss -->|Close| CloseModal[Close modal & reset alerts]
    UserDismiss -->|Cancel| CloseModal
    
    DisableSave --> UserCancels{User clicks Cancel?}
    UserCancels -->|Yes| CloseModal
    UserCancels -->|No| UserInteract
    
    CloseModal --> End
```

## Diagram 2

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Closed: Initial State
    
    Closed --> Opening: show=true
    Opening --> Loaded: subscriptionDetails loaded
    Opening --> Loading: isSubscriptionLoading=true
    
    Loading --> Loaded: Data fetched
    Loading --> Error: subscriptionRequestError=true
    
    Loaded --> Editing: User interacts
    
    Editing --> Editing: Toggle checkboxes
    Editing --> Editing: Edit email
    Editing --> Editing: Edit phone
    Editing --> ValidForm: All inputs valid
    Editing --> InvalidForm: Validation fails
    
    InvalidForm --> Editing: User corrects
    ValidForm --> Saving: User clicks Save
    
    Saving --> Success: subscriptionUpdateSuccess=true
    Saving --> Failed: subscriptionUpdateError=true
    
    Success --> Closed: User closes modal
    Failed --> Editing: User retries
    Error --> Closed: User closes modal
    
    ValidForm --> Closed: User clicks Cancel
    InvalidForm --> Closed: User clicks Cancel
    Loaded --> Closed: User clicks Cancel
    
    Closed --> [*]
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant User
    participant AlertMeModal
    participant Redux
    participant API
    
    User->>AlertMeModal: Opens modal (show=true)
    AlertMeModal->>Redux: useSelector(getUserPreferences)
    Redux-->>AlertMeModal: userPreferences
    
    alt subscriptionDetails exists
        AlertMeModal->>AlertMeModal: Set mode=UPDATE
        AlertMeModal->>AlertMeModal: Load existing subscription
    else no subscription
        AlertMeModal->>AlertMeModal: Set mode=SAVE
        AlertMeModal->>AlertMeModal: Set defaults from preferences
    end
    
    AlertMeModal->>User: Display form
    
    User->>AlertMeModal: Toggle email checkbox
    AlertMeModal->>AlertMeModal: Update subscriptionLocal.enable_email
    AlertMeModal->>AlertMeModal: Validate email
    
    User->>AlertMeModal: Enter email address
    AlertMeModal->>AlertMeModal: Update subscriptionLocal.recipient_email
    AlertMeModal->>AlertMeModal: Validate with isValidEmail()
    
    User->>AlertMeModal: Toggle SMS checkbox
    AlertMeModal->>AlertMeModal: Update subscriptionLocal.enable_sms
    
    User->>AlertMeModal: Enter phone number
    AlertMeModal->>AlertMeModal: Update subscriptionLocal.mobile_number
    AlertMeModal->>AlertMeModal: Validate with isPossiblePhoneNumber()
    
    User->>AlertMeModal: Toggle platform checkbox
    AlertMeModal->>AlertMeModal: Update subscriptionLocal.enable_platform
    
    User->>AlertMeModal: Click Save
    AlertMeModal->>AlertMeModal: hasVinSubscriptionChanged()
    
    alt mode=UPDATE and all disabled
        AlertMeModal->>API: unsubscribe(subscribeeDetails, subscriptionLocal)
        API-->>AlertMeModal: Response
    else mode=SAVE
        AlertMeModal->>API: subscribe(subscribeeDetails, subscriptionLocal)
        API-->>AlertMeModal: Response
    else mode=UPDATE
        AlertMeModal->>API: updateSubscription(subscribeeDetails, subscriptionLocal)
        API-->>AlertMeModal: Response
    end
    
    AlertMeModal->>AlertMeModal: setShowAlert(true)
    
    alt Success
        AlertMeModal->>User: Show success alert
    else Error
        AlertMeModal->>User: Show error alert
    end
    
    User->>AlertMeModal: Close modal
    AlertMeModal->>AlertMeModal: onModalClose()
    AlertMeModal->>User: Modal hidden
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class AlertMeModal {
        +show: bool
        +hide: func
        +modalSize: string
        +headerText: string
        +bodyText: string|node
        +emailText: string
        +textMessageText: string
        +platformNotificationText: string
        +subscribeeDetails: object
        +displayedId: string
        +isSubscriptionLoading: bool
        +subscriptionDetails: object
        +subscriptionRequestError: bool
        +updateSubscription: func
        +subscribe: func
        +unsubscribe: func
        +context: object
        +isSubscriptionUpdating: bool
        +subscriptionUpdateSuccess: bool
        +subscriptionUpdateError: bool
        -mode: string
        -subscriptionLocal: object
        -showAlert: bool
        -showSubscriptionRequestAlert: bool
        +requiresApproval()
        +emailIsNotApproved()
        +smsIsNotApproved()
        +isSubscriptionPending()
        +hasVinSubscriptionChanged()
        +isEmailSubscriptionInvalid()
        +isMobileSubscriptionInvalid()
        +onSave()
        +onModalClose()
    }
    
    class SubscriptionLocal {
        +enable_email: bool
        +enable_sms: bool
        +enable_platform: bool
        +recipient_email: string
        +mobile_number: string
        +requires_approval: bool
        +context: object
    }
    
    class MODES {
        <<enumeration>>
        SAVE
        UPDATE
    }
    
    AlertMeModal --> SubscriptionLocal: manages
    AlertMeModal --> MODES: uses
```
